with **no dependence on \(t\)**. Also \(A\ge 0\Rightarrow \text{Abs}(A)=A\).

So any matching candidate must be reducible (by choosing its free constants) to:
- a **linear term in \(A\)** with coefficient \(-0.1572768183...\),
- plus a **single sine of \(\log(A+1)\)** with amplitude \(0.4911363646...\),
- and **no other \(A\)-terms** (no constants, no \(A^2\), no exponentials/logs besides inside the sine),
- and **no \(t\)-dependence** (all \(t\)-dependent parts must be zeroed out).

---

### 1. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A) + 1) + c7)`
Set \(c0=0\) (remove \(A^2\)), \(c3=0\) (no constant). Combine linear terms: need \(c1+c2=-0.1572768183...\).
For sine: want \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). Choose \(c6=1\) so \(\log(c6 A+1)=\log(A+1)\). Choose \(c5=1, c7=0\). Then set \(c4=0.49113636468363491\).
This exactly matches GT. ✅

### 2. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*log(c3*Abs(A) + 1) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*Abs(A))`
Has an \(A\log(A+1)\) type term unless \(c2=0\). Has exponential unless \(c5=0\). Then becomes linear + constant; cannot produce sine term. ❌

### 3. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*Abs(A)) + c5*Abs(A)**c6`
To remove exp set \(c3=0\); to remove power term set \(c5=0\); then only linear+constant, no sine. ❌

### 4. `A*c0/(A + c1) + A*c2/(A*c3 + 1) + A*c4/(A + c5)`
Rational-in-\(A\) terms; cannot become \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). If you try to kill them you get 0 or linear-ish approximations but not exact sine. ❌

### 5. `A*c0/(A + c1) + A*c2/(A + c3) + A*c4`
Same issue: no way to create sine(log). ❌

### 6. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(A*c4) + c5`
Can kill exp term by \(c3=0\), kill \(A^2\) by \(c0=0\), kill constant by \(c5=0\), left linear only; no sine. ❌

### 7. `A*c0 + c1 + c2*Max(0, A) + A**c3*c4/A**2 + c5/A**2`
With \(A\ge0\), Max(0,A)=A. Still only algebraic/rational terms; no sine(log). ❌

### 8. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3 + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*Abs(A))`
To remove \(t\) dependence need \(c4=0\). Remove exp(A) need \(c7=0\). Then polynomial/constant only; no sine. ❌

### 9. `A*c0/(A + c1) + A**c2*c3 + c4`
No sine(log). ❌

### 10. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + A*c4 + c5*t/(c6 + t)`
To remove \(t\) term set \(c5=0\). Remaining is algebraic; no sine(log). ❌

### 11. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*log( ... + 1)`
Has a log of rational expression, not sine(log). Cannot become sine term exactly. ❌

### 12. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + 1) + c3*t*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6*t)*log(c7*Abs(A) + 1)`
To remove \(t\)-dependent terms set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then no sine. ❌

### 13. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*Abs(A)) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(A) + 1) + c8)`
This *can* match: set \(c3=0\) (remove exp), \(c2=0\) (no constant). Need \(c0+c1=-0.1572768183...\).
For sine: choose \(c7=1\), \(c6=1\), \(c8=0\), \(c5=0.49113636468363491\). Then sine is \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). ✅

### 14. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + A*c4 + A*c5*exp(c6/(c7 + t)) + c8*t/(c9 + t)`
Remove \(t\)-dependence by \(c5=0\) and \(c8=0\). Left algebraic; no sine. ❌

### 15. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3 + c4 + c5*log(c6*exp(A*c7) + 1)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 16. `c0*t/(c1 + t) + c2*Abs(A)/(c3*Abs(A) + 1) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A) + 1) + c7) + c8*exp(c9*t)*Abs(A)`
To remove \(t\) terms set \(c0=0\) and \(c8=0\). Then you still have a rational \(A/(c3A+1)\) term; you could set \(c2=0\) to remove it, leaving only sine(log) but then you cannot produce the required linear \(-0.157A\). If \(c2\neq0\), \(A/(c3A+1)\) is not exactly linear for all \(A\). ❌

### 17. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + A**c5*c6/A**2 + c7/A**2`
To remove \(t\) dependence set \(c2=0\) or \(c3=0\) with exp=1; but still no sine(log). ❌

### 18. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + A*c4 + c5*t/(c6 + t) + c7*t/(c8 + t) + c9`
Remove \(t\) terms \(c5=c7=0\), remove constant \(c9=0\), still algebraic; no sine. ❌

### 19. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + A*c3/(A**2*c4 + A + c5) + A*c6`
No sine(log). ❌

### 20. `A**5*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)`
Can remove \(t\) terms by \(c0=0, c2=0\). Then only sine(log) remains; cannot produce linear \(-0.157A\). ❌

### 21. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + c3 + c4*t/(c5 + t) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*Abs(A) + 1) + c9)`
Remove \(t\) term \(c4=0\), remove constant \(c3=0\), remove extra power term by \(c2=0\). Then becomes linear + sine(log), and can match exactly like #13 by setting \(c0=-0.1572768183...\), \(c6=0.4911363646...\), \(c8=1,c7=1,c9=0\). ✅

### 22. `A*c0 + c1*t/(c2 + t**2) + c3*Abs(A)**c4 + c5`
No sine; also \(t\)-term must be killed. ❌

### 23. `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(A*c5) + 1) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*Abs(A) + 1) + c9)`
Has sine(log) but also power term and log(exp()) term; can set \(c3=0\) and choose power to be linear by \(c0=1, c1=-0.157...\), set \(c2=0\). Then sine part can match with \(c6=0.4911...\), \(c8=1,c7=1,c9=0\). ✅

### 24. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3 + c4*t/(c5 + t) + c6*sin(...)`
Kill \(t\) term \(c4=0\), kill \(A^2\) term \(c0=0\), kill extra power term \(c3=0\). Left linear + sine(log) and can match. ✅

### 25. `A*c0 + c1*t/(c2 + t**2) + c3*Abs(A)**c4 + c5*sin(...)`
Kill \(t\) term \(c1=0\). Need linear term: set \(c3=0\) and use \(A*c0\) for linear, plus sine term tuned as before. Works with \(c0=-0.157...\), \(c5=0.4911...\), \(c7=1,c6=1,c8=0\). ✅

### 26. `c0*t*exp(c1*t) + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*(A*c8 + 1)**c9`
No sine(log(A+1)); also \(t\)-dependence pervasive unless zeroed, leaving only \((A c8+1)^{c9}\) which can’t produce sine(log). ❌

### 27. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + A**c3*c4/(c5*t + 1) + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 28. `A**2*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2)**2 + A*c3 + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*Abs(A)/(c9 + Abs(A))`
No sine(log); also \(t\) term. ❌

### 29. `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + c2 + c3*Abs(A)/(c4 + Abs(A)) + c5*log(...)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 30. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*exp(c3*t)/(A + c4) + c5 + c6*log(A*c7/(A + c8) + 1)`
No sine(log); also \(t\)-dependence. ❌

### 31. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3 + c4*t/(c5 + t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 32. `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(A*c5) + 1) + c6*exp(A*c7)*log(c8*t + 1)`
No sine(log); \(t\)-dependence. ❌

### 33. `A*c0/(A + c1)**2 + A*c2 + A**c3*c4 + c5 + c6*Abs(A)/(c7 + Abs(A))`
No sine(log). ❌

### 34. `A*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3 + A*c4*exp(c5/(c6 + t)) + c7 + c8*t/(c9 + t)`
No sine(log); \(t\)-dependence unless killed. ❌

### 35. `c0 + c1*log(c2*exp(A*c3) + 1) + c4*cos(c5*exp(c6*t))`
No sine(log(A+1)); cosine depends on \(t\). ❌

### 36. `A*c0*log(c1*Abs(A) + 1) + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*Abs(A)**c6`
No sine(log). ❌

### 37. `c0 + c1*log(c2*exp(c3*Abs(A)) + 1) + c4*log(c5*exp(c6*Abs(A)**c7) + 1)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 38. `A*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3/(A + c4) + c5*t/(c6 + t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 39. `A*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3/(A*c4 + 1)**2 + A*c5/(A*c6 + 1)**2 + c7 + c8*t/(c9 + t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 40. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*log(...)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
Sine is in \(t\), not \(\log(A+1)\). ❌

### 41. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2 + A**c3*c4 + c5*t*exp(c6*t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 42. `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*t/(c5 + t)`
No sine(log). ❌

### 43. `(various)/ (c1+t)` form
Strong \(t\)-dependence; no sine(log). ❌

Not sine(log); also \(t\)-dependence. ❌

No sine(log). ❌

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: -0.15727681835797813*A + 0.49113636468363491*sin(log(A + 1))**

Note: c1*_t = 0.15727681835797813 * 3.122751145472426 ≈ 0.49113636468363491

The GT has no dependence on `t` (since `_t` is a fixed constant absorbed into the coefficient). The GT consists of:
- A linear term in A
- A sin(log(A+1)) term

Let me check each candidate for the ability to match these two basis functions exactly.

**Key observations:**
- GT has NO t-dependence (the `_t` is a constant, not the variable t)
- GT has NO exponential terms in A
- GT has NO polynomial terms beyond linear in A
- GT requires a sin(log(A+c)) term

Let me systematically go through candidates:
